msg:We highly recommend Shantou International Hotel.

The hotel room is very spacious, clean and comfortable. The hotel room has all the modern and necessary amenities.  No need to bring adaptor and there is plenty USB ports.

The hotel itself has many restaurants providing quality and variety.  We dine at the Taichi dim sum restaurant...very nice.

Hotel is 15mins from Shantou Railway station, making it convenient for those coming from high speed rail. It is within walking distance from Longyan food street and major shopping centres ie Mixc and Sunning.  It is also near to tourist attractions.

Most of all, we are so impressed with the staff.  They are professional,  proactive, helpful and warm.  This is consistent throughout all levels of the staff.  The reception staff even come out of the counter to help us with the Alipay app.  Shantou has no subway so very important to be able to use the app to hail taxi.

Thank you Shantou international hotel and especially its staff, for making our stay so comfortable and memorable üòÄ

msg:Although the hotel has been renovated, the basics are still there, the facilities and services are average, and the rooms are small. There are two advantages: 1. The robot delivering food is very interesting, and the children are very interested in it. For this reason, they even ordered two takeaways for the robot to deliver upstairs. 2. Breakfast is in the revolving restaurant on the top floor, and the location is very good. Let‚Äôs talk about the bigger disadvantages: 1. Breakfast is free for children under 80 centimeters tall. Only infants under 80 centimeters are allowed, okay? ! 2. The parking spaces are very limited, so I endured it; I parked in the narrow underground parking lot of the hotel on the first night and was scratched on the roof of my car, so I endured it; later, there was no parking space for me to park in the cinema square next door, so I endured it; I had to pay the parking fee first. Then I went to the front desk to get the tickets and went to the cinema parking lot to refund the money. I really felt that it was unnecessary and weird, so I couldn't bear it. 3. The third shortcoming is intolerable. For breakfast on the last day, I used a stirring stick in a jar on the table to drink coffee. It was a plastic stirring stick with a round handle on the top. What I always understood was that this kind of plastic stirring stick It was a one-time use. Who would have thought that when the waiter came to collect the dishes, he took the stirring stick that I had put aside and wiped it with a napkin, then put it back in the jar with the stirring stick on the table... I suddenly felt like It's disgusting. I wonder if the stirring stick I just used was in the mouth of another guest and stained with other guests' saliva... As a five-star hotel, is this the level of hygiene? It's so disgusting... At this point, we feel we must give it a negative review. I don‚Äôt know where so many good reviews come from? !
